TB00153 DECISION REGISTER v1_70
OPEN DECISIONS REQUIRING BILL RATIFICATION
============================================================

============================================================
1. PURPOSE
============================================================

This register enumerates every open decision surfaced
during TB00153 master-defect-register compilation that
requires Bill ratification BEFORE the TB00154+ diagram-
rework session sequence can proceed without ambiguity.

Each entry presents:
  - Decision title and DCN reference
  - Status (OPEN — awaiting Bill ratification)
  - First-principles framing of the choice
  - Claude's recommendation with data justification
  - Alternative(s) considered with trade-off analysis
  - Bill action required (single-line directive form)
  - Downstream impact if deferred

Per TB00152 NSI v1_0 §4.4, this register is one of the
four required TB00153 planning deliverables.

Per TB00000 v2_20 §X (engineering authority): Claude is
the engineering authority and produces analysis +
recommendation. Bill ratifies decisions; Bill does not
perform the engineering analysis.

DEC-014  1011002 WS_Manager_Coding_Spec dv1_26
         retirement under DEC-012 / DD-012 campaign
         methodology
------------------------------------------------------------

STATUS: RATIFIED — executed across TB00261-TB00298-
TB00299; S-6 governance updates closed at TB00299.

ORIGIN SESSION: TB00299 (S-6 closure entry). Cascade
execution spanned TB00261 (Phase 0 scope-quantification
audit; logged as DR-055 in MDR v1_21) through TB00298
(S-1 Phase 1 gap-audit; TB00208 v1_0 authoring) through
TB00299 (S-4 retirement + S-5 cascade-anchor revision +
S-6 governance updates). Decision authorized by
DEC-012(a) original AA=10 campaign authorization at
TB00190 which enumerated 1011002 as a candidate in the
12-spec AA=10 retirement list. TB00208 §5.6 explicitly
specified the DEC-NEW entry for this cascade per the
paired-DEC pattern established at TB00207 §5.6 +
DEC-013 at TB00297.

FIRST-PRINCIPLES FRAMING:

Per §4.5 DD-012 v2_38 0500000-canonical-all-docs scope:
where 0500000 diagrams encode an architectural element
(in this case mod:WS_Manager across Tier 1 Context +
D1 R5 Kraken WS Connection Architecture + D5 R6 + D7 R5
Dispatch Seam), the subordinate spec (1011002 WS_Manager_
Coding_Spec) is DUPLICATIVE not COMPLEMENTARY. The
duplicative spec is retired; the diagram is the canonical
record. 1011002 dv1_26 contained:
  - Bucket (a) ARCHITECTURAL RESTATEMENT — ~95 elements
    restating WS Manager architecture (connection state,
    token management, keepalive, zombie detection,
    sequence gap detection, per-pair instrument status
    cache, candle-close detection, startup warm-up +
    indicator seeding, mid-session reconnect, Pending
    Order Registry, drawdown state, Selection Controller
    state, WS dispatch routing). All canonical at 0500000
    dv1_78 D1 R5 + D7 R5 + Tier 1 Context + §8
    architectural rules (AR-015 + AR-020 + AR-039 +
    AR-044 + AR-045 + AR-052 + AR-053 + AR-056 + AR-068
    + AR-073 + AR-074).
  - Bucket (b) CODING-UNIQUE — ~35 elements migrated to
    0511001 dv1_9 parent WS_Manager_Specification via
    PROSE-UPDATE-A through PROSE-UPDATE-J ten-PROSE-
    UPDATE cluster across the dv1_7-dv1_8-dv1_9 chain
    PRIOR to this cascade's S-1 audit.
  - Bucket (c) ARCHITECTURAL CONTENT NOT IN DIAGRAMS —
    0 elements. All four cluster gaps from prior TB00194
    pre-DD-012 gap register CLOSED in current canonical
    baselines (cluster C1 per-module wallet parameter
    registry; cluster C2 per-wallet drawdown halt
    machine; cluster C3 R:R-driven sizing curve form
    factor; cluster C4 HR-WM-034 prose-narration gap).
    S-2 NO-OP.

DECISION:

    DEC-012 6-sub-step methodology:

    S-1 audit         CLOSED TB00298 (TB00208 v1_0
                      Phase 1 Gap Register).
    S-2 amendments    NO-OP (bucket (c) empty; cluster
                      C1-C4 gaps closed in prior diagram
                      increments).
    S-3 gap-fill      CLOSED PRIOR to this cascade in
                      0511001 dv1_7 -> dv1_8 -> dv1_9

                      WM-* identifiers present in dv1_9
                      at expected line numbers (HR-WM-

(b) NOTE: DEC-014 is the SECOND paired top-level DEC
    entry created at the Decision Register layer for a
    retirement-cascade closure (after DEC-013 for
    0811001 at TB00297). The paired-DEC pattern was
    established at TB00207 §5.6 (0811001 cascade) and
    continues for the 1011002 cascade per TB00208 §5.6
    explicit specification. Prior AA=10 cascade closures
    (DR-044 through DR-056) followed an MDR-only pattern
    without paired DEC entries; the paired-DEC pattern
    is the post-DEC-013 forward standard.

S-5 ANCHOR-IDENTIFICATION CORRECTION RECORD:

TB00299 NSI v1_0 §3.4 and TB00208 v1_0 §5.5 both cited
"0510000 System_Components_Anchor" as the S-5 anchor
target for this cascade. Per DCN AABCDDD governance
(0311001 v1_18 §11 sub-domain anchor child-document
inventory rules):
  1011002 = AA=10 B=1 C=1 DDD=002
  -> parent anchor = 1010000 (AA=10 B=1 C=0 DDD=000).
  0510000 = AA=05 B=1 anchor for 0511001-0511006
  (does not contain 1011002 reference).
Pattern precedent: 0811001 retirement (TB00295-TB00296
cascade) amended 0810000 (AA=08 B=1 anchor). The correct
S-5 anchor for the 1011002 retirement cascade is
1010000. Correction enacted under RR-SCOPE-005
derivable-decision authority + RR-SCOPE-007 v2_30
SELF-AUTHORED-NSI-SOURCE-PROHIBITION (NSI/TB00208
sentences had no Bill-quote backing) + DD-011 v2_38
FP/DP-derivability-test gate (Option B single compliant
remaining option; OUTCOME 1 derivable). The TB00208
v1_0 + TB00299 NSI v1_0 authoring defects are
forensically recorded but preserved byte-identical in
git history; no retroactive amendment to those documents
is required.

FIRST-PRINCIPLES FRAMING:

Per §4.5 DD-012 v2_38 0500000-canonical-all-docs
scope, DD-012 methodology produces DISPOSITION
CLASSIFICATION (RETIRE or PRESERVE), NOT a retirement
funnel. The methodology audits a subordinate spec
against canonical 0500000 architectural content and
determines whether the spec is duplicative
(architectural restatement -> RETIRE) or
complementary (external-fact-contract or coding-
unique content -> PRESERVE). The classification
depends on the structural character of the audited
spec.

0411001 Kraken_WS_v2_Specification dv1_12 is a WIRE-
CONTRACT / EXTERNAL-FACT-CONTRACT specification
documenting Kraken WebSocket v2 protocol facts:
  - WebSocket endpoints (Kraken-defined).
  - JSON message schemas for public channels
    (instrument, status, ohlc, ticker, book) and
    private channels (executions, balances).
  - Authentication protocol (Kraken-required REST
    GetWebSocketsToken sequence).
  - Wire-protocol pitfalls (Kraken-imposed:
    underscore-vs-hyphen stp_type form, tick_size
    deprecation, edit_order deprecation).
  - JSON formats for outbound messages (add_order,
    amend_order, batch_add, cancel_order,
    batch_cancel).
  - Rate limit numerics (2.34/sec decay, 80 orders
    per pair, tier-dependent maxratecount).
  - Connection management protocol (application JSON
    ping 30s + zombie detection 90s + reconnect
    scenarios A/B).
  - Python library configuration (websockets asyncio
    client max_size, open_timeout, max_queue,
    ping_interval).

These facts are NOT TothBot architectural decisions
— they are external constraints imposed by Kraken's
wire protocol surface. 0500000 dv1_78 encodes TothBot
architectural decisions (mod:WS_Manager + ar:AR-001..
074 + rule:HR-WM-021..034 + contract:WM-PACE-001/
WM-PACE-002 + contract:WM-SHARD-001/WM-SHARD-010 +
contract:WM-RECONNECT-016 + decision:D-03/D-06/D-08
etc.). 0500000 should NOT encode Kraken external
protocol surface; that is by design.

The relationship between 0411001 and 0500000 is
BIDIRECTIONAL CITATION (0500000 defines AR-NNN
architectural authorities for WS-layer concerns;
0411001 implements those authorities as wire-
contract rules with explicit "(AR-NNN)" citations
on individual WS-NNN rules). 0411001 cites ~30
canonical 0500000 ARs (AR-001, AR-007, AR-008,
AR-009, AR-021, AR-022, AR-023, AR-024, AR-026,
AR-027, AR-028, AR-029, AR-030, AR-031, AR-032,
AR-033, AR-034, AR-037, AR-038, AR-039, AR-040,
AR-041, AR-046, AR-047, AR-050, AR-057, AR-058,
AR-059, AR-061, AR-064). Each citation marks the
canonical 0500000 architectural authority that the
wire-contract rule implements. Citation pattern is
CORRECT under DD-002 prose-follows-diagram.

DD-012 v2_38 retirement-gate FP/DP analysis per
TB00211 §4.3 enumerated four options:
  Option A (RETIRE 0411001; migrate wire-contract
    content into 0500000) — REJECTED. Forcing
    external Kraken protocol facts into the TothBot
    architectural anchor violates 0500000 scope.
    0500000 owns TothBot architecture; Kraken wire
    surface is out of scope.
  Option B (RETIRE 0411001; migrate to residual
    AA=10 coding spec) — REJECTED. AA=10 coding
    specs are subordinate to architectural sources,
    not authoritative external-fact records. AA=10
    container for external Kraken facts is the same
    structural defect as Option A.
  Option C (RETIRE 0411001; author new AA=04 parent
    spec) — REJECTED. Zero content migration —
    0411001 IS the wire-contract target. A new
    AA=04 parent would simply be a renamed 0411001.
  Option D (PRESERVE 0411001) — ACCEPTED. Single
    compliant option DERIVABLE under DD-011 v2_38
    FP/DP-derivability-test. 0411001 is the
    authoritative wire-contract specification for
    Kraken WebSocket v2 protocol; PRESERVE preserves
    the external-fact contract for code authoring.

DECISION:

  0411001 PRESERVED. AA=04 sub-campaign
  scope-determination established: subordinate AA=04
  specs documenting external Kraken protocol facts
  (wire-contract / fee-rate / REST API facts) are
  STRUCTURALLY DISTINCT from AA=08 / AA=10
  subordinate specs that restate 0500000
  architectural content. AA=04 subordinate specs
  are PRESERVE candidates by structural character.

FIRST-PRINCIPLES FRAMING:

Per §4.5 DD-012 v2_38 0500000-canonical-all-docs
scope, DD-012 methodology produces DISPOSITION
CLASSIFICATION (RETIRE or PRESERVE), NOT a retirement
funnel. 0411002 Kraken_REST_API_Specification dv1_1
is a WIRE-CONTRACT / EXTERNAL-FACT-CONTRACT
specification documenting Kraken REST API protocol
facts:
  - REST endpoint URIs (Kraken-defined:
    /0/private/GetWebSocketsToken, /0/public/OHLC,
    /0/private/OpenOrders, /0/private/Balance,
    /0/private/CancelAllOrdersAfter,
    /0/public/SystemStatus, /0/private/QueryOrders,
    /0/public/Ticker).
  - HTTP request/response wire format (Kraken-imposed
    nonce + signature + API-key headers; JSON
    response envelope with error[] + result{}
    schemas).
  - Authentication signature algorithm (Kraken-
    defined HMAC-SHA512 over nonce + POST data with
    URI prefix).
  - Error code taxonomy (Kraken-defined EGeneral /
    EAPI / EOrder / ETrade / EQuery / EService
    namespaces).
  - Python aiohttp library configuration (ClientSession
    + ClientTimeout + TCPConnector parameter VALUES).
  - Endpoint-specific contract details (OHLC
    response[-1] exclusion at dv1_6; QueryOrdersInfo
    targeted single-order reconciliation; Ticker
    liquidity probe at universe load for DEFECT-SS-006
    closure at dv1_1).

These facts are EXTERNAL CONSTRAINTS imposed by
Kraken's REST API surface. They are not TothBot
architectural decisions. The structural relationship
between 0411002 and 0500000 is BIDIRECTIONAL CITATION
identical to 0411001/DEC-018 finding: 0500000 dv1_78
§4 AR registry defines TothBot architectural rules
(AR-017 / AR-021 / AR-025 / AR-031 / AR-035 / AR-036
/ AR-037 / AR-038 for REST-layer architecture);
0411002 dv1_1 implements those ARs as REST wire-
contract rules and CITES the AR authorities via
"(AR-NNN)" inline references. This is the CORRECT
relationship per DD-002 prose-follows-diagram.

DD-012 v2_38 retirement-gate FP/DP analysis per
TB00212 §4.3 enumerated four options (A RETIRE -> 0500000
diagrams / B RETIRE -> residual AA=10 spec / C RETIRE
-> 0410000 anchor / D PRESERVE). Options A/B/C
eliminated on first-principles grounds (forcing
external Kraken REST protocol facts into TothBot
architectural anchor / coding spec / sub-domain anchor
violates 0500000 scope, AA=10 subordination, or
namespace hierarchy respectively). Option D PRESERVE
single compliant option DERIVABLE under DD-011 v2_38
FP/DP-derivability-test.

FP/DP ANALYSIS OUTCOME — OPTION 5 CODING START SELECTED.

First-principles framing:
  The project mission is profit maximization and loss
  minimization via trading (TB00000 §1.2 + 0911001
  dv1_1 §2). Diagrams are INSTRUMENTAL — they exist to
  enable correct code. Code that doesn't get written
  produces zero profit and zero loss minimization.
  Every session spent on diagram refinement that isn't
  catching real coding-blocking ambiguity is delayed
  mission progress.

V-040 IV at 100% closure (TB00384) means every component
already answers TB00000 §3.2 Q1-Q5 from diagrams alone.
DD-014 v2_57 PRE-EMIT SCAN authorization gate is MET.
V-041 (producer-consumer binding declarations; 119
catalogued FAILs in TB00362 v1_1) and V-042 (event-
stream coherence; 30 Class B + 4 Class A FAILs in
TB00363 v1_0) are REFINEMENT not BLOCKERS — the
underlying Q1-Q5 answerability passed V-040 IV without
them.

Per Deming §6.7 "Use data, not narrative": let coding
generate the empirical data on which diagram gaps
actually matter. Stop speculating; start measuring.

    work not on critical path; 6+ sessions of deferred
    mission progress against speculative coding-blocker

DEC-039 records Bill's ratification (at TB00396) of Option A
for the scope of the 0500000 Consolidation Campaign. The
TB00396 NSI had scoped Phase 1 as "migrate parameter VALUES
out of TB00000 sec 9.17 into the 0500000 diagram notes, then
RETIRE the sec 9.17 entry." Bill challenged this on the
established testing-vs-architecture separation. The decision:
  Option A (CHOSEN) — separate architecture from testing.
    Only ARCHITECTURAL content (component existence,
    ownership, contracts, information flows, gates, regimes,
    channels, module structure) migrates into 0500000.
    Parameter STARTING VALUES are transient testing seeds
    (per TB00000 sec 9.16 + sec 6.8 every starting value
    except the sacred 1:1.5 R:R floor is temporary, CIATS-
    owned, and replaced by paper-trading data); they stay
    permanently in TB00000 sec 9.17. 0500000 records the
    architectural FACT that a parameter exists and who owns
    it (CIATS), never the transient numeric value. TB00000
    sec 9.17 is the permanent canonical parameter registry
    and is NOT retired by the campaign.
  Rejected alternative — the dv1_0 / TB00396-NSI scope
    "migrate values then retire sec 9.17." Migrating
    transient values into the canonical 0500000 diagrams
    would pollute the highest-cost architecture source with
    frequently-changing content, make 0500000 stale the
    instant CIATS changes a value, and reintroduce the
    prose-driven-error class the campaign exists to
    eliminate — merely relocated into the diagrams.

"migrate values then retire sec 9.17" scope. It does NOT
supersede DEC-038 (the Phase 0 D8 token-registration choice,
which was independently consistent with Option A: that
session registered the architectural fact of the two D8 caps
and migrated no value).

SUB-GROUP SCOPE / ONE-DIAGRAM DISCIPLINE. The sec 9.17 group is

DEC-068: UNIFIED OCS 4-PHASE MODEL ADOPTED AS THE CANONICAL
         PHASE STRUCTURE OF THE 0500000 CONSOLIDATION
         CAMPAIGN (0911002) - SUPERSEDES THE OLD 5-PHASE
         NUMBERING - companion to the 0911002 dv1_3 -> dv1_4
         plan amendment

STATUS: RATIFIED. Recorded at TB00470 (Bill OCS chat-turn
directive: amend 0911002 to adopt the unified OCS 4-phase
model). The model itself was Bill-ratified at the register
level at TB00394 v1_1 (TB00469) sec PHASE-MODEL; DEC-068 is
the Decision-Register authority record for adopting it as the
governing phase structure of plan 0911002.

DECISION: the 0500000 Consolidation Campaign uses the unified
OCS 4-phase model:
  Phase 0  SCOPE DEFINITION (the TB00394 register; document-
           level MOVE/STAY/SPLIT; RATIFIED at TB00394 v1_1).
  Phase 1  ELEMENT AUDIT (per-document, element-level, DD-012
           element identification; one source doc per session
           per RR-SCOPE-011; NOT started).
  Phase 2  DD-012 THREE-BUCKET CLASSIFICATION + SEQUENCING

OLD-NUMBERING -> UNIFIED-MODEL MAP (canonical; mirrors
TB00394 v1_1 sec PHASE-MODEL):
  old 0911002 Phase 0 (D8-closure) ........ CLOSED HISTORY
  old Phase 1 (CIATS-ownership attestation) Phase 3 EXECUTION
  old Phase 2 (AA=05 component specs) ...... Phase 3 / E1
  old Phase 3 (AA=04/06/07/08 instance) .... Phase 3 / E2
  old Phase 4 (anchor/domain collapse) ..... Phase 3 / E3

RATIONALE. The TB00394 register (Phase 0 scope-definition
deliverable) was authored against the unified model at
TB00469, but plan 0911002 still carried the old 5-phase
numbering, leaving the governing plan and its Phase 0
deliverable inconsistent. A single canonical phase model
across the plan and register removes the drift class this
campaign exists to eliminate. The old Phase 4 (anchor/domain
collapse) is folded into Phase 3 as sub-stage E3 because it
is execution work that depends on every E1/E2 migration and
retirement; the old Phase 1 (CIATS-ownership attestation) is
a diagram-amendment activity and is therefore Phase 3
EXECUTION (consistent with the TB00394 v1_1 sec 9.17-source
classification "sec 9.17 completion occurs in Phase 3
execution"); the old Phase 0 (D8 thread closure, TB00395) is
retained as CLOSED HISTORY (the migration-pattern seed case),
not as the new Phase 0 (which is document-level scope
definition). The E1 -> E2 -> E3 sub-stage order preserves
the original dependency order (component specs before
instance specs before anchor/domain collapse).

DEC-066 is the authority record for HOW EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED is
integrated into 0500000 without conflicting with the DEC-065
ratified 7-value enum. Bill's directive this session: keeping
EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED is SETTLED; "keep" / "remove" are rejected
framings. The correct questions are WHERE it belongs and HOW it
is integrated conflict-free. FP/DP outcome:

WHERE. EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED already belongs to layer:L3_Emergency_SL
- the off-book emergency stop-market resting on
container:Matching_Engine (ar:AR-008 crash protection only). Its
home and its bus interface already exist in 0500000 D3: the L3
desc produces evt:TRADE_CLOSE -> contract:CIATS_Trade_Outcome_Bus
with the record "emitted on TothBot recovery / WS reconnect via
channel:kraken_ws_executions exec_type=trade backfill." No new
diagram and no new interface element are required for conflict-
free integration.

WHAT THE CONFLICT WAS. An authorship error, not a missing home:
the D3 exit_controller_owner q5_logs falsely listed
EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED among the reasons mod:Exit_Controller emits,
contradicting the same element's q1_do ("L3 emergency SL is off-
book Kraken-side crash protection only and is NOT owned by Exit
Controller runtime"), compounded by the stale L1a signal enum
(SIGNAL_DECAY / MOMENTUM_LOSS).

HOW (the ratified resolution) - PRODUCER-PARTITION the bus
exit_reason field. Two producers feed the one
contract:CIATS_Trade_Outcome_Bus:
  Producer 1 = mod:Exit_Controller -> the seven normal-operation
    values (DEC-065): { TP_FILL, MAE_THRESHOLD_BREACH,
    HTF_REGIME_REVERSAL, DAILY_REGIME_DOWNGRADE, TIME_EXPIRY,
    TP_PARTIAL_FILL_REMAINDER, PAIR_LIMIT_ONLY_EXIT }.
  Producer 2 = layer:L3_Emergency_SL -> EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED,
    emitted via crash-recovery reconciliation (executions backfill
    on TothBot recovery / WS reconnect).
EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED is a legitimate bus exit_reason from the
recovery producer and is explicitly OUTSIDE the Exit-Controller
7-value set. D3 dv1_130 renders this: the owner q5_logs now lists
the 7-value set plus an explicit producer-partition note; the L3
element retains EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED as its own produced reason.

RELATION TO DEC-065. DEC-065 Q1 listed EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED among
"stale signal-based names ... mid-consolidation drift to be
reconciled (0911002 sec 5A Track A)." DEC-066 records the
reconciliation outcome and does NOT re-open Q1/Q2/Q3: SIGNAL_DECAY
is re-homed (Q2), MOMENTUM_LOSS is removed/superseded by the
regime triggers EC-L1A-001/002/003, but EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED is
RETAINED and producer-partitioned - it was never an Exit-
Controller normal-operation reason, so it is neither "stale" nor
"removed," it is correctly re-attributed to its L3 recovery
producer.

CARRY-FORWARD. A dedicated Emergency-SL crash-recovery diagram
(full Reconciliation_REST detect-on-restart recovery mechanics)
would add DD-014 design-completeness value but is NOT necessary
for conflict-free integration; building it now would violate one-
diagram-per-session (RR-SCOPE-011 / DEC-003 Path A). Deferred as
a future DD-014 / Track-A item.

DEC-065 is the authority record for the canonical shared
exit_reason enum and the disposition of SIGNAL_DECAY. The three
decisions were ratified by Bill at TB00442 (SL sec 3) and are
recorded here so the enum has a permanent Decision-Register home
independent of the session log. They are NOT re-opened by any
session executing the 0911002 sec 5A reconciliation cascade.

Q1 RATIFIED. The canonical shared exit_reason List-A base is
the SIX regime-based values:
  { TP_FILL, MAE_THRESHOLD_BREACH, HTF_REGIME_REVERSAL,
    DAILY_REGIME_DOWNGRADE, TIME_EXPIRY,
    TP_PARTIAL_FILL_REMAINDER }
These are the values rendered canonically at 0500000 D5/D6 and
in 0511004 dv1_7 (regime-based exit design). They supersede the
stale signal-based names (SIGNAL_DECAY / MOMENTUM_LOSS /
EMERGENCY_SL_FIRED) still rendered at D3, which is mid-
consolidation drift to be reconciled (0911002 sec 5A Track A),
not a conceptual defect.

Q3 RATIFIED. PAIR_LIMIT_ONLY_EXIT is kept as a legitimate 7th
exit_reason value, CIATS-owned for tracking. Source: 0511004
dv1_7 sec 5 (AR-040 pair-status adaptation, line 320) - an
exchange-state-forced exit when a pair goes limit_only while a
position is open (cancel TP; IOC limit sell at best_bid). Its
two siblings PAIR_CANCEL_ONLY_HOLD / PAIR_MAINTENANCE_HOLD
(lines 326/331) are log-events (position HELD, not exited) and
are NOT exit_reason values. The canonical shared exit_reason
enum is therefore SEVEN values:
  { TP_FILL, MAE_THRESHOLD_BREACH, HTF_REGIME_REVERSAL,
    DAILY_REGIME_DOWNGRADE, TIME_EXPIRY,
    TP_PARTIAL_FILL_REMAINDER, PAIR_LIMIT_ONLY_EXIT }

Q2 RATIFIED. SIGNAL_DECAY is NOT an exit_reason value. It is
re-homed as a PENDING-ENTRY-ORDER CANCEL TRIGGER (CIATS-owned):
if the entry signal (SSS) deteriorates below threshold while the
entry order is still working (unfilled / partially filled),
cancel the unfilled / remaining qty; the Exit Controller owns
any already-filled portion per the existing AR-054 partial-fill
handling. TB00442 SL sec 2.4 confirmed this mechanism does NOT
exist in the current entry criteria - it is net-new design to be
authored into 0511003 Execution_Engine + 0711001 SSS_Signal_
Model. SIGNAL_DECAY is REMOVED from the LG-TOB-002 / exit enum.
Tracked as CF-TB00442-A; sequenced as 0911002 sec 5A Track B
(separate from the Track A reconciliation cascade).

forbids re-opening Q1/Q2/Q3 and forbids diagram/spec edits this

S-2 DECISION (Bill ratification gate). The 10 protocol-fact rules
are the only items not landed in 0500000. The gate question: do
they BLOCK 0511001 retirement (Option B) or do they have a
